<p><span class="font6">Te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">miliki prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in yang le</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">bih tinggi dibandingkan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas kimpul te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi, dimana prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas kimpul te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi masing-masing se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 19,17% dan 5,09%. Yudistira (2016) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rta He</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rviandri dan Wardana (2018) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyatakan bahwa se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi kadar prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in, maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rasan produk. Prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngalami de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">naturasi saat prose</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">s pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">manasan suhu tinggi kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na mudahnya ikatan hidroge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">n be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rstruktur he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">liks untuk putus, hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ncari air untuk me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngganti ikatan yang putus (Sari, 2018). Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lanjutnya, prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in akan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ntuk matriks yang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngikat air, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga air akan sulit ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">luar (Mishartina </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">l al</span><span class="font6">., 2018). Matriks prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in akan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rte</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mu de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pati dan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ntuk matriks pati-prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in yang stabil de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan ikatan kovale</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">n, ikatan hidroge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">n, dan rantai ionik, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga matriks pati-prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in ini me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan produk pangan yang dihasilkan ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ras kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rjadi inte</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">raksi antara gugus amino prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan gugus hidroksil pati me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lalui ikatan hidroge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">n (Brigita, 2021). Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin banyak prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in, maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin banyak matriks pati-prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in yang te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ntuk se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan produk se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ras.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Fracture</span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"> (Daya Patah)</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan hasil sidik ragam, pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">fracture</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6"> (daya patah) </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">. Nilai daya patah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 3,04 N sampai 10,72 N. Nilai daya patah te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1 (90% TTT: 10% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 3,04 N yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C2, C3, C4, dan C5, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai daya patah te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C5 (50% TTT: 50% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 10, 72 N yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1, C2, C3, dan C4. Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">iring be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtambahnya rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas kimpul te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi, maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah daya patah </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">baliknya se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">iring be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtambahnya rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai daya patah </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Daya patah sangat pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nting guna me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">tahui karakte</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ristik te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kstur dari se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">gi ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rapuhan (Barre</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">tt, 1998). Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai daya patah, maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin sulit suatu produk untuk dipatahkan. Pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatan nilai daya patah dise</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatkan kadar prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">. Nilai daya patah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbanding lurus de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan nilai ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rasan, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah yang ditambahkan maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rasan, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi daya patah </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">. Hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but dise</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rikatan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan air, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga air me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">njadi sulit me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nguap saat prose</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">s pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">manasan dan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cilnya rongga udara yang te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ntuk (Imandira &amp;&nbsp;Ayustaningwarno, 2013). Te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbatasnya rongga udara yang ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cil me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan produk sulit untuk me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbang dan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kstur me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">njadi ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ras dan sulit dipatahkan (Ramadhani </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">., 2022). Pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">litian ini se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">jalan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">litian Anugrahati dan Widjanarko (2021) yang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatan prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatan daya patah. Ole</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na itu, daya patah sangat be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kstur </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">, kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na nilai daya patah yang se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cil me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cil gaya yang dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlukan untuk me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">matahkan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kstur </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyah (Le</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">stari, 2019).</span></p>
<h2><a name="bookmark25"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;"><a name="bookmark26"></a>Crunchiness</span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"> (Kerenyahan)</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan hasil sidik ragam, pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">crunchine</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6"> (ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan) </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">. Nilai ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 22,22 N sampai 44,73 N. Nilai ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C5 (50% TTT: 50% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 22,22 N yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C2, C3, C4, dan C5, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1 (90% TTT: 10% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 44,73 N yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C2, C3, C4, dan C5. Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">iring be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtambahnya rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas kimpul te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi maka akan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatkan ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">baliknya se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">iring be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtambahnya rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah maka me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nurunkan ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tidak re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyah.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas kimpul te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi pada </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tingginya nilai ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">baliknya se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkurangnya nilai ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">. Hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but dise</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rasan dan nilai daya patah maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah nilai ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan. Rosida (2021) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyatakan bahwa se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin banyak pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nambahan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung atau pati te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi yang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngandung pati re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">siste</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">n akan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatkan tingkat</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan. Hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but didukung ole</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">litian Cakrawati &amp;&nbsp;Mujdalipah (2014) yang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyatakan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rat pangan golongan pati re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">siste</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">n dapat me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbantu me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbaiki te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kstur dan ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">cookie</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">s </span><span class="font6">dibandingkan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nambahan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rat pangan yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rsumbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">r dari se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">alia.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Kadar amilosa juga dapat me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan produk. Te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas kimpul te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">autoclavingcooling</span><span class="font6"> me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngandung amilosa se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 29,96% (Wiadnyani </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">., 2017), se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">dangkan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngandung amilosa se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 39% (Manoppo, 2012). Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah makan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkurang ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">. Kadar amilosa dalam bahan pangan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi hasil produk de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan daya pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cah yang baik kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rikan sifat ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ras se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndapatkan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kstur re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyah. Namun, apabila kadar amilosa te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlalu tinggi dalam bahan maka te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rjadi pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbatasan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbangan granula kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtahankan inte</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">gritas granula, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkurang ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyahannya kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na produk tidak me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbang se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpurna.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Chewiness</span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"> (Daya Kunyah)</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">che</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">wine</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6"> (daya kunyah) </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">. <p><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1 (90% TTT: 10% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 17,22 N yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C2, C3, C4, dan C5, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">che</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">wine</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss </span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C5 (90% TTT: 10% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 53,63 N yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1, C2, C3, dan C4. Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">iring be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtambahnya rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas kimpul te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah daya kunyah </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">baliknya se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">iring be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtambahnya rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi daya kunyah </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">Che</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">wine</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6"> (daya kunyah) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan banyaknya e</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rgi yang dibutuhkan untuk me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngunyah makanan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lum dite</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lan, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai che</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">wine</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ss maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin banyak e</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rgi yang dibutuhkan untuk me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngunyah (Sabe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ri </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">., 2021). Hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but dise</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah yang tinggi dapat me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatkan kandungan prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in yang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan tingginya nilai </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">che</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">wine</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6">, maka hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan tingginya nilai </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">che</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">wine</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss </span><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mbutuhkan e</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rgi untuk me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngunyah. <p><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Cohesiveness</span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"> (Daya Kohesif)</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">cohe</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">sive</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ne</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6"> (daya kohe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sif) </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">. Nilai rata-rata diikuti ole</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h huruf yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da pada kolom yang sama me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da nyata (P&lt;0,05)</span></p>

<p><span class="font6">Shaliha </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">. (2017) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyatakan bahwa daya kohe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sif me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nggambarkan ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kompakan atau ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">utuhan suatu produk, dimana se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">cohe</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">sive</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ne</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6">, maka produk se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin kompak. Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah pada </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6">, maka se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai daya kohe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sif. Te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah tinggi akan kadar prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in dan amilosa yang dapat me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngikat air. Se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah, maka kadar air </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> ikut me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkat. Hawthornthwaite</span><span class="font0">i </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al.</span><span class="font6"> (2015) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyatakan bahwa daya kohe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sif produk ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ring se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cara signifikan sangat dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi ole</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h kadar air walaupun pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">daannya sangat ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cil. Pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">hardne</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6"> dan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">cohe</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">sive</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ne</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6"> juga se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">jalan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatan kadar air (Indiarto </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">., 2012). Air te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but dapat me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkuat ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kuatan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngikat yang dibutuhkan untuk me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">katkan bahan-bahan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">njadi satupadu, dimana produk yang dihasilkan akan le</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">bih kompak. Ole</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na itu, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi rasio te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah, maka prote</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">in dan amilosa se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin banyak me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngikat air dan baku dapat le</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">bih re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kat me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">njadi satu,</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kompakan atau daya kohe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sif </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> ikut me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkat.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;">Hasil Analisis Uji Warna</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap nilai rata-rata L*, a*, b*, dan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">browning inde</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">x </span><span class="font6">(inde</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ks ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">coklatan) non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rs. Nilai rata-rata L*, a*, b*, dan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">browning inde</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">x</span><span class="font6"> (inde</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ks ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">coklatan) dapat dilihat pada Tabe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">l 4.</span></p>
<p><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;">Koordinat L* (Lightness)</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">l 4. nilai L* me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngalami pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nurunan, dimana nilai L* </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 35,93 sampai 66,84. <p><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai L* te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1 (90% TTT :10% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 66,84 yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C2, C3, C4, dan C5. Nilai L* (</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">lightne</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">ss</span><span class="font6">) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyatakan ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ce</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rahan warna, dimana se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin tinggi nilai L*, maka</span></p>
<p><span class="font4">Itepa: Jurnal Ilmu dan Teknologi Pangan, Anna Yasmin Saragih dkk. /Itepa 12 (4) 2023 900-921 </span><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin &nbsp;ce</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah &nbsp;warna yang dihasilkan</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">(Sinaga, 2019). Pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nurunan nilai L* </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> dise</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na adanya prose</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">s </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">maillard</span><span class="font6"> se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">hingga warna </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin ge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lap </span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;">Koordinat a*</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">Dapat dilihat pada Tabe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">l 4. bahwa te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rjadi pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatan nilai a*. Hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but didukung ole</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">litian Putri </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">. &nbsp;(2016) yang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nyatakan bahwa</span></p>

<h2><a name="bookmark27"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark28"></a>Koordinat b*</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan Tabe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">l 4. &nbsp;&nbsp;te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rjadi</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatan nilai b*. Nilai b* </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 29,83 sampai 39,30. Nilai b* te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1 (90% TTT :10% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 29,83</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">yang be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C3, C4, dan C5, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">dangkan nilai a* te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C5 (50% TTT :50% TKM) &nbsp;&nbsp;se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar &nbsp;&nbsp;39,30 yang &nbsp;&nbsp;be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da</span></p>

Pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ningkatan nilai b* me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nandakan warna se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin kuning. Hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but dise</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan kare</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">na pra-pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lalui &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;prose</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">s &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndaman &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;yang</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nye</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">babkan warna kuning akan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nguat se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lah pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">manasan (Pangastuti </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">., 2013) </span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Browning Index</span></p>

<p><span class="font6">dihasilkan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">makin ge</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lap (Pangastuti </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">e</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">t al</span><span class="font6">., 2013). <h2><a name="bookmark29"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark30"></a>Warna</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan hasil sidik ragam, te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap warna </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> pada uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik. Nilai uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik warna be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 1,30 sampai 4,40. Nilai uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik warna te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C5 (50% TTT: 50% TKM) se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 1,30 de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan krite</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ria tidak suka dan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1, C2, C3, dan C4. Nilai uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik warna te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C3 (70% TTT: 30% TKM) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h angka 4,40 de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan krite</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ria agak suka dan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1, C2, C4, dan C5. Be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan hasil uji warna de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">colorime</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">te</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">r </span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C3 me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">miliki nama warna </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">potte</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs clay</span><span class="font6">, de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan nilai L* 48,00, a* 7,30, b* 34,67. Adapun nilai </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs </span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C3 adalah 68,55. <h2><a name="bookmark31"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark32"></a>Aroma</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan hasil sidik ragam, pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah tidak be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&gt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap aroma </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> pada uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik. <h2><a name="bookmark35"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark36"></a>Rasa</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap rasa </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> pada uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik. Nilai uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik rasa be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 1,95 sampai 4,25. Nilai uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik rasa te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C5 (50% TTT: 50% TKM) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h angka 1,95 de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan krite</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ria tidak suka dan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1, C2, C3, dan C4.</span></p>
<h2><a name="bookmark37"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark38"></a>Tabe</span><span class="font0" style="font-weight:bold;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;">l 6. <p><span class="font6">Nilai uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik rasa te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C3 (70% TTT: 30% TKM) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h angka 4,25 de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan krite</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ria agak suka dan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1, C3, dan C4. <h2><a name="bookmark39"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark40"></a>Penerimaan Secara Keseluruhan</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Hasil sidik ragam me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rmodifikasi dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruh nyata (P&lt;0,05) te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rhadap pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rimaan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cara ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">luruhan </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> pada uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik. Pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rimaan ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">luruhan ini dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngaruhi ole</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rimaan lainnya, se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rti warna, aroma, te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">kstur, dan rasa. Nilai uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rimaan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cara ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">luruhan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkisar antara 1,40 sampai 4,40. Nilai uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ne</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rimaan se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cara ke</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">luruhan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">re</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ndah dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C5 (50% TTT: 50% TKM) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h angka 1,40 de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan krite</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ria tidak suka dan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1, C2, C3, dan C4. Nilai</span></p>
<p><span class="font6">uji he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik warna te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h dari pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C3 (70% TTT: 30% TKM) me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">mpe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h angka 4,40 de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan krite</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ria agak suka dan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">da signifikan de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C1, C2, C4, dan C5.</span></p>
<h2><a name="bookmark41"></a><span class="font6" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark42"></a>Karakteristik Kimia Produk Terbaik</span></h2>
<p><span class="font6">Pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbaik </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> dite</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ntukan be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan uji se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nsoris se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">cara he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik. Be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rdasarkan uji se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nsoris he</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">donik, </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan nilai te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rtinggi dipe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">role</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h ole</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">h pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan C3 (70% TTT: 30% TKM). Nilai rata-rata karakte</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ristik kimia pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbaik dapat dilihat pada Tabe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">l 6. </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">Non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rlakuan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbaik de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngandung kadar air se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 2,71% dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">lah me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nuhi syarat SNI 2973:2018 (Biskuit), dimana maksimal kadar air te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkandung adalah 5%. Kadar se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rat pangan total yang te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rkandung dalam </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span><span class="font6"> te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbaik de</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">ngan pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rbandingan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung talas dan te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">pung kacang me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rah adalah se</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">be</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">sar 4,88 g pe</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">r 100 g. Hal te</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">rse</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">but me</span><span class="font0">i</span><span class="font6">nunjukkan bahwa </span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">non-flaky cracke</span><span class="font0" style="font-style:italic;">i</span><span class="font6" style="font-style:italic;">rs</span></p>
